\DoxyCodeLine{02924                 lineno = self.gds\_get\_node\_lineno\_()}

\DoxyCodeLine{02926                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \textcolor{keyword}{False}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02927             value = value}
\DoxyCodeLine{02928             enumerations = [\textcolor{stringliteral}{'yes'}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{'no'}]}

\DoxyCodeLine{02932                 result = \textcolor{keyword}{False}}
